They are also responsible for safeguarding the assets\nof the Company and hence for taking reasonable steps for the prevention and\ndetection of fraud and other irregularities.\n\n\n', u'3\n', u'\n', u' PAGEBREAK ', u'\n', u'\n', u'Table of Contents', u'\n', u'\n', u'\n', u'\n', u'\n', u'Independent auditors\x92 report to the members of M (2003)\xa0plc', u'\n', u'\xa0\n\n', u'We have audited the financial statements of M (2003)\xa0plc for the year ended\n31 March\xa02004 which comprise the profit and loss account, the balance sheets,\nthe cash flow statement, the statement of total recognised gains and losses,\nthe reconciliation of movements in shareholders\x92 interests, the statement of\naccounting policies, the reconciliation of net cash flow movements in net\nmonetary funds and the related notes 1 to 26. Our audit work has been undertaken\nso that we might state to the Company\x92s members those matters we are required\nto state to them in an auditors\x92 report and for no other purpose. To the\nfullest extent permitted by law, we do not accept or assume responsibility to\nanyone other than the Company and the Company\x92s members as a body, for our\naudit work, for this report, or for the opinions we have formed.\n\n\n', u'Respective responsibilities of directors and auditors', u'\n', u'As described in the Statement of directors\x92 responsibilities, the Company\x92s\ndirectors are responsible for the preparation of the financial statements in\naccordance with applicable United Kingdom law and accounting standards. Our responsibility is to audit the financial statements in\naccordance with relevant United Kingdom legal and regulatory requirements and\nauditing standards.\n\n\n', u'We report to you our opinion as to whether the financial statements give a true\nand fair view and whether the financial statements have been properly prepared\nin accordance with the Companies Act 1985. An audit includes examination, on a\ntest basis, of evidence relevant to the amounts and disclosures in the\nfinancial statements. It also includes an assessment of the significant\nestimates and judgements made by the directors in the preparation of the\nfinancial statements and of whether the accounting policies are appropriate to\nthe circumstances of the Company and the Group, consistently applied and\nadequately disclosed.\n\n\n', u'We planned and performed our audit so as to obtain all the information and\nexplanations which we considered necessary in order to provide us with\nsufficient evidence to give reasonable assurance that the financial statements\nare free from material misstatement, whether caused by fraud or other\nirregularity or error. u'\xa0\xa0\xa0', u'Restructuring', u'\n', u'In respect of the year ended 31 March\xa02003 and until 19 May\xa02003, the Company\nwas the ultimate holding company for the Marconi Group. Under the schemes of\narrangement of Marconi Corporation plc and the Company, pursuant to Section\n425 of the Companies Act 1985 which became effective on 19 May\xa02003, Marconi\nCorporation plc issued new share capital and cancelled the old shares held by\nthe Company. Therefore the Company ceased to be the ultimate holding company\nof the Marconi Group on 19 May\xa02003 and all activities have therefore been\ndisclosed as discontinued. Trading in the Company\x92s shares on the London\nStock Exchange ceased on 16 May\xa02003 and the Company\x92s shares were\nsubsequently delisted.\n\n\n', u'On 19 May\xa02003 the Company, as a result of the shares it held in Marconi\nCorporation plc being cancelled, divested fully of its interests in the\nMarconi Group for nil proceeds. This resulted in a gain of \xa33,386\xa0million on\nthe transfer of ownership of the Marconi Group being equivalent to its\nconsolidated net liabilities. On the same date, the scheme of arrangement of\nMarconi Corporation plc came into effect resulting in an \xa3804\xa0million\nreceivable from the Marconi Group being waived by the Company and its\nsubsidiary undertakings.\n\n\n', u'Pursuant to the Company\x92s Scheme, the remaining assets of the Company will be\ndistributed over time to its creditors, following which it is intended that the\nCompany will be liquidated or dissolved. There will be no circumstances in\nwhich any value will be returned to shareholders under the terms of the\nCompany\x92s Scheme.\n\n\n', u'Consequently, the Group after 19 May\xa02003 consists of the Company and its\nnon trading and dormant subsidiaries Ancrane, M Ansty Limited, M Nominees Limited, Photoniqa Limited and Yeslink Unlimited.\n\n\n', u'2', u'\xa0\xa0\xa0', u'Accounting policies', u'\n', u'The financial statements have been prepared in accordance with accounting\nstandards applicable in the UK.\n\n', u'The more important Group accounting policies are summarised below to facilitate\nthe interpretation of the financial statements.\n\n\n', u'Accounting convention', u'\n', u'The financial statements are prepared under the historical cost convention, as\nmodified by the valuation of listed current and fixed asset investments.\n\n\n', u'Basis of consolidation', u'\n', u'The financial statements consolidate the accounts of the Company and all\nof its subsidiary undertakings (Group companies or subsidiaries). All\ninter-company balances and transactions have been eliminated upon\nconsolidation.\n\n\n', u'Turnover', u'\n', u'Turnover excludes VAT and comprises sales to outside customers. Revenue from\nproduct sales of hardware and software is recognised when persuasive evidence\nof an arrangement exists, delivery has occurred or service has been rendered,\ncustomer acceptance has occurred, the Group\x92s price to the buyer is fixed or\ndeterminable, and collectability is reasonably assured. Revenue from services\nis recognised at the time of performance and acceptance by the customer.\n\n', u'Revenue from multiple element contracts is allocated based on the fair value of\neach individual element.\n\n\n', u'Revenue on long-term contracts is recognised under the\npercentage-of-completion method of accounting and is calculated based on the\nratio of costs incurred to date compared with the total expected costs for\nthat contract.\n\n\n', u'Currency translation', u'\n', u'Transactions denominated in foreign currencies are translated into the\nfunctional currency at the rates ruling at the dates of the transactions.\nMonetary assets and liabilities denominated in foreign currencies at the\nbalance sheet date are retranslated at the rates ruling at that date. These\ntranslation differences are dealt with in the profit and loss account with\nthe exception of certain gains and losses arising under hedging\ntransactions as described below.\n\n\n', u'Profits and losses of overseas subsidiaries, joint ventures and associates and\ncash flows of overseas subsidiaries are translated at the average rates of\nexchange during the year. Non-sterling net assets are translated at year end\nrates of exchange. Key rates used are as follows:\n\n', u'\n', u'\n', u' Begin Table Head ', u'\n', u'\xa0', u'\n', u'\xa0', u'\n', u'\xa0', u'\n', u'\xa0', u'\n', u'\xa0', u'\n', u'\xa0', u'\n', u'\xa0', u'\n', u'\xa0', u'\n', u'\xa0', u'\n', u'\xa0', u'\n', u'\xa0', u'\n', u'\xa0', u'\n', u'\xa0', u'\n', u'\xa0', u'\n', u'\xa0', u'\n', u'\xa0', u'\n', u'\xa0', u'\n', u'\n', u'\n', u'\xa0', u'\n', u'\xa0', u'\n', u'Average rates', u'\n', u'\xa0', u'\n', u'Year-end rates', u'\n', u'\n', u'\n', u'\xa0', u'\n', u'\xa0', u'\n', u'2004', u'\n', u'\xa0', u'\n', u'2003', u'\n', u'\xa0', u'\n', u'2004', u'\n', u'\xa0', u'\n', u'2003', u'\n', u'\n', u' End Table Head ', u'\n', u' Begin Table Body ', u'\n', u'\n', u'US dollar', u'\n', u'\xa0', u'\n', u'\xa0', u'\n', u'1.7023', u'\n', u'\xa0', u'\n', u'\xa0', u'\n', u'\xa0', u'\n', u'1.5538', u'\n', u'\xa0', u'\n', u'\xa0', u'\n', u'\xa0', u'\n', u'1.8379', u'\n', u'\xa0', u'\n', u'\xa0', u'\n', u'\xa0', u'\n', u'1.5807', u'\n', u'\xa0', u'\n', u'\n', u'\n', u'Euro', u'\n', u'\xa0', u'\n', u'\xa0', u'\n', u'1.4435', u'\n', u'\xa0', u'\n', u'\xa0', u'\n', u'\xa0', u'\n', u'1.5499', u'\n', u'\xa0', u'\n', u'\xa0', u'\n', u'\xa0', u'\n', u'1.4956', u'\n', u'\xa0', u'\n', u'\xa0', u'\n', u'\xa0', u'\n', u'1.4486', u'\n', u'\xa0', u'\n', u'\n', u' End Table Body ', u'\n', u'\n', u'The differences arising from the restatement of profits and losses and the\nretranslation of the opening net liabilities to year end rates are taken to\nreserves.\n\n\n', u'9\n', u'\n', u' PAGEBREAK ', u'\n', u'\n', u'Table of Contents', u'\n', u'\n', u'Notes to the accounts ', u'continued\n\n\n', u'\xa0\n\n\n', u'2', u'\xa0\xa0\xa0', u'Accounting policies ', u'continued\n\n\n', u'Acquisitions and disposals', u'\n', u'On the acquisition of a business, including an interest in an associated\nundertaking, fair values are attributed to the Group\x92s share of separable net\nassets. Where the cost of acquisition exceeds the fair values attributable to\nsuch net assets, the difference is treated as purchased goodwill and\ncapitalised in the balance sheet in the year of acquisition.\n\n\n', u'The profit or loss on the disposal or closure of a previously acquired business\nincludes the attributable amount of any purchased goodwill relating to that\nbusiness not previously charged to the profit and loss account.\n\n\n', u'The results and cash flows relating to a business are included in the\nconsolidated profit and loss account and the consolidated cash flow statement\nfrom the date of acquisition or up to the date of disposal.\n\n\n', u'Financial instruments', u'\n', u'Prior to the financial restructuring the Group has used financial instruments,\nincluding interest rate swaps, currency swaps and other derivatives, solely for\nthe purposes of raising finance for its operations and managing interest and\ncurrency risk associated with the Group\x92s underlying business activities. There\nis no trading activity in financial instruments.\n\n\n', u'Hedges of the net investment in overseas subsidiaries', u'\n', u'The Group\x92s policy has been to finance where possible its activities in the\nsame currencies as those used for its foreign investments in order to hedge\nforeign currency exposure of net investments in foreign operations. This\npolicy is implemented by financing in the related currency.\n\n\n', u'Exchange gains or losses arising on the hedging borrowings are dealt with as\na movement in reserves, to the extent they offset losses or gains on the\nhedged investment.\n\n\n', u'Equity forward contracts', u'\n', u'The Group established three trusts for the purchase of shares and\nshare-related instruments for the benefit of employees \x97 the Marconi Employee\nTrust (MET), the GEC Employee Share Trust and the GEC Special Purpose Trust.\nThese trusts, from 19 May\xa02003, are consolidated in the financial statements\nof Marconi Corporation plc.\n\n\n', u'The independent trustee of the MET, Bedell Cristin Trustees Limited, entered\ninto contracts (the Equity Forward Contracts) to hedge the potential cost of\nthe Group\x92s share plans. These contracts were closed out on 19 May\xa02003. The\nagreed settlement amount of \xa335\xa0million was classified as a provision within\nthe Group\x92s balance sheet at 31 March\xa02003 and utilised in the year ended 31\nMarch\xa02004.\n\n\n', u'Interest rate risk exposure', u'\n', u'Prior to the financial restructuring, it has been Group policy to hedge its\nexposure to movements in interest rates associated with its borrowing primarily\nby means of interest rate swaps. Payments and receipts under interest rate swap\nagreements specifically designated for hedging purposes are recorded in the\nprofit and loss account on an accruals basis. Gains and losses arising on\ntermination of hedging instruments where the underlying exposure remains are\nrecognised in the profit and loss account over the remaining life of the\nhedging instrument.\n\n\n', u'Tangible fixed assets', u'\n', u'Property, plant, machinery, fixtures, fittings, tools and equipment are\nrecorded at cost and depreciated on a straight-line basis over their\nestimated useful lives from the time they are brought into use. Freehold land\ndoes not bear depreciation where the original cost of purchase was separately\nidentified. Provision is made for any impairment.\n\n\n', u'Tangible fixed assets are depreciated using the following rates:\n\n', u'\n', u'\n', u' Begin Table Head ', u'\n', u'\xa0', u'\n', u'\xa0', u'\n', u'\xa0', u'\n', u'\n', u' End Table Head ', u'\n', u' Begin Table Body ', u'\n', u'\n', u'Freehold buildings\n', u'\n', u'\xa0', u'\n', u'\x97 2% to 4% per annum', u'\n', u'\n', u'\n', u'Leasehold property\n', u'\n', u'\xa0', u'\n', u'\x97 over the period of the lease or 50\xa0years for long leases', u'\n', u'\n', u'\n', u'Plant and machinery\n', u'\n', u'\xa0', u'\n', u'\x97 10% per annum on average', u'\n', u'\n', u'\n', u'Fixtures, fittings, tools and equipment\n', u'\n', u'\xa0', u'\n', u'\x97 10% per annum', u'\n', u'\n', u' End Table Body ', u'\n', u'\n', u'Leased assets', u'\n', u'Assets held under finance leases and other similar contracts, which confer\nrights and obligations similar to those attached to owned assets, are\ncapitalised as tangible fixed assets and are depreciated over the shorter of\nthe lease terms and their useful lives. The capital elements of future lease\nobligations are recorded as liabilities, while the interest elements are\ncharged to the profit and loss account over the period of the leases to produce\na constant rate of charge on the balance of the capital repayments outstanding.\nHire purchase transactions are dealt with similarly except that assets are\ndepreciated over their useful lives.\n\n\n', u'Rentals under operating leases are charged on a straight-line basis over the\nlease term, even if the payments are not made on such a basis.\n\n\n', u'10\n', u'\n', u' PAGEBREAK ', u'\n', u'\n', u'Table of Contents', u'\n', u'\n', u'2', u'\xa0\xa0\xa0', u'Accounting policies ', u'continued\n\n\n', u'Goodwill', u'\n', u'Purchased goodwill is capitalised and amortised on a straight-line basis over\nits estimated useful economic life. Each acquisition is separately evaluated\nfor the purposes of determining the useful economic life, up to a maximum of\n20\xa0years. The useful economic lives are reviewed annually and revised if\nnecessary. Provision is made for any impairment.\n\n\n', u'Research and development', u'\n', u'Expenditure incurred in the period is charged against profit unless\nspecifically chargeable to and receivable from customers under agreed\ncontract terms.\n\n\n', u'Stock', u'\n', u'Stock is stated at the lower of cost and net realisable value. Provision is\nmade for obsolete, slow-moving or defective items where appropriate.\n\n\n', u'Contracts in progress', u'\n', u'Profit on long-term contracts in progress is taken when a sale is recorded on\npart-delivery of products or part-performance of services, provided that the\noutcome of the contract can be assessed with reasonable certainty. Amounts\nrecoverable on long-term contracts, which are included in debtors, are stated\nat the net sales value of the work done less amounts received as progress\npayments on account. Excess progress payments are included in creditors as\npayments received in advance. Cumulative costs incurred net of amounts\ntransferred to cost of sales, less provision for contingencies and anticipated\nfuture losses on contracts, are included as long-term contract balances in\nstock.\n\n\n', u'Warranties', u'\n', u'Provisions for estimated expenses related to product warranties are made at\nthe time products are sold. These estimates are established using historical\ninformation on the nature, frequency, and average cost of warranty claims.\n\n\n', u'Taxation', u'\n', u'Taxation on profit on ordinary activities is that which has been paid or\nbecomes payable in respect of the profits for the year. Deferred taxation is\nprovided in full on timing differences that result in an obligation at the\nbalance sheet date to pay more tax, or a right to pay less tax, at a future\ndate, at rates expected to apply when they crystallise based on current tax\nrates and law. Timing differences arise from the inclusion of items of income\nor expenditure in taxation computations in periods different from those in\nwhich they are included in the financial statements. Deferred tax assets are\nrecognised to the extent that it is regarded as more likely than not that they\nwill be recovered. Deferred tax assets and liabilities are not discounted.\n\n\n', u'Investments', u'\n', u'Joint ventures comprise long-term investments where control is shared under a\ncontractual arrangement. The sector analysis of turnover, profit and net assets\nexcludes the Group\x92s share of the results and net assets of joint ventures.\nAssociates consist of long-term investments in which the Group holds a\nparticipating interest and over which it exercises significant influence.\nInvestments in joint ventures and associates are stated at the amount of the\nGroup\x92s share of net assets including goodwill at the balance sheet date\nderived from audited or management accounts made up to that date. Loss before\ntaxation includes the Group\x92s share of joint ventures and associates.\n\n\n', u'Other unlisted fixed asset investments are stated at cost less provision\nfor impairment in value. Listed fixed asset investments are stated at\nmarket value.\n\n\n', u'Investments in the Company\x92s shares, held within the GEC Employee Share\nTrust and the MET, are included on the Group balance sheet at cost, less\nprovision for impairment.\n\n\n', u'Pensions and other post retirement benefits', u'\n', u'The operating cost of providing pensions and other post retirement benefits,\nas calculated periodically by independent actuaries, is charged to the\nGroup\x92s operating profit or loss in the period that those benefits are earned\nby employees. The financial return expected on the pension schemes\x92 assets is\nrecognised in the period in which they arise as part of finance income and\nthe effect of the unwinding of the discounted value of the pension schemes\nliabilities is treated as part of finance costs. The changes in value of the\npension schemes\x92 assets and liabilities are reported as actuarial gains or\nlosses as they arise in the consolidated statement of total recognised gains\nand losses. The pension schemes\x92 surpluses, to the extent they are considered\nrecoverable, or deficits are recognised in full and presented in the balance\nsheet net of any related deferred tax.\n\n\n', u'Share options', u'\n', u'The costs of awarding shares under employee share plans are generally charged\nto the profit and loss account over the period to which the performance\ncriteria relate. During the year to 31 March\xa02004 the profit and loss account\nhas also been charged with interest arising on the Equity Forward Contract\nwhich hedges the share options. When share options granted lapse, any\nassociated costs that were treated as cost of acquisition are credited to\neither goodwill, or to the profit and loss account if there is no remaining\ngoodwill.\n\n\n', u'As a result of the financial restructuring, the Company\x92s shares have been\ndelisted.
